After waiting for 40 minutes, at 12:36, the hotel lobby duty manager on that day called me back (the last number of the mobile phone was 0782), saying that the hotel could not check the surveillance video, and the hotel staff could not enter the monitoring room! ! ! If the hotel staff could not enter the monitoring room, how to deal with the emergency? After I said that I could not accept this result, the lobby duty manager suggested that I call the police! ! ! It was the hotel who took the initiative to suggest that I call the police! In fact, it was not a big deal, but the attitude of the hotel on the side made me a little serious.
At this time, I asked the higher-level leaders of the hotel to come forward to solve this problem. At my strong request, the hotel front office manager called me at 12:52 (the last number was 6258), saying that she understood the matter and asked me to wait patiently, and she would solve the problem that the hotel could not enter the monitoring room to check the video. Then it was a really long wait. I strolled around Qinghui Garden and ate Wumi Congee, but I didn't get a call back. It wasn't until I couldn't wait any longer and was already on my way to the hotel that the manager called me back at 15:10, saying that they could finally enter the monitoring room and asked me to wait for them to check the surveillance video. I said it was okay, I would be at the hotel soon, and I wanted to check the video together. Let's watch the video first at the hotel.
The most outrageous thing happened after I arrived at the hotel. I arrived at the hotel lobby at 15:30. After a few minutes, the front office manager came over with a security guard and told me: They watched the entrance video of my car entering the parking lot at 12:55 and 21:03 the day before, and confirmed that my car had scratches when it entered. At the same time, they couldn't let me go into the monitoring room to watch the video, and they wouldn't send me videos or photos to show me. Anyway, they confirmed that there were scratches when I came, but there was no video or photo proof. I wanted to see the general manager of the hotel, but I was not allowed to. The security manager didn't show up. If I want to see the photos, I hope I call the police, and the police can go into the monitoring room to watch the video. The hotel showed an attitude that I don't mind making a big deal out of it!
Okay! Then we'll call 110. When the police arrived, they also showed an attitude that they couldn't trust the hotel after hearing what happened. They thought it was a simple matter that could be solved by showing me the video, but they had to call the police. Seeing the police coming, the hotel agreed to let the police enter the monitoring room to watch the video, and at first they couldn't let the police take pictures of the video to show me! ! ! At my insistence and the request of the police, they agreed to take pictures of the video. The police showed me two photos of entering the parking lot entrance from the monitoring room. The photos were not clear, and the police couldn't see clearly whether there were any scratches. This was what the hotel and the security guard from the security department told me before. They clearly saw obvious scratches when I entered the parking lot! They have always been shirking their responsibilities! It has nothing to do with the hotel! But I didn't say anything about the hotel? I just hope the hotel can help me check the surveillance to see what happened! ! ? At this time, I showed the police the photo of me parking in the parking space, hoping to check the video of the first half-hour parking in the basement (I only listened to the first half-hour parking, and went out after checking in). The police understood me very well and entered the monitoring room again. As a result, he came out in one minute and told me that the monitoring room said that there was no video storage, and there was no video storage for yesterday's monitoring. It cannot be viewed! The hotel has violated the law. Do you know it yourself? ? ? The state stipulates that hotel surveillance videos must be stored for at least 90 days! Does the hotel management have legal knowledge? There is not even a 24-hour storage video? ! 
The matter cannot be resolved here. I left the hotel at 5 pm. I just wanted to make a phone call and hope that the hotel could help me check the video. I had already left the hotel and did not think that the car being scratched had anything to do with the hotel. And a small scratch is not serious. But what happened in the next six hours made me speechless about the attitude of the hotel management in handling things. 
Please note that all guests who have checked in or are about to check in this high-end hotel cannot guarantee your safety at present. Because the hotel has not even met the national laws.
